<script>
//========== 쿠키값 처리 함수 S
function getCookieVal (offset) {
    var endstr = document.cookie.indexOf (";", offset);
    if (endstr == -1)
        endstr = document.cookie.length;
    return unescape(document.cookie.substring(offset, endstr));
}

function GetCookie (name) {
    var arg = name + "=";
    var alen = arg.length;
    var clen = document.cookie.length;
    var i = 0;
    while (i < clen) {	//while open
        var j = i + alen;
        if (document.cookie.substring(i, j) == arg)
            return getCookieVal (j);
        i = document.cookie.indexOf(" ", i) + 1;
        if (i == 0)
            break;
    }	//while close
    return null;
}
function GetAuthCookie(name) {
    var cookies = document.cookie;
    var value  = "";
    if(cookies.indexOf(name) != -1) {
        var start = cookies.indexOf(name) + name.length + 1;
        var end   = cookies.indexOf(";",start);

        if(end == -1) end = cookies.length;

        value = cookies.substring(start,end);
        value = unescape(value);
    }

    return value;
}
//========== 쿠키값 처리 함수 E

//로그인
function loginFrame () {
    //페이지 URL
    var returl = document.location;
    if (returl == null || returl == ""){
        returl = M_SITE;
    }
    returl = escape(returl);

    var login_url = "https://membership.chosun.com/login/protect_sso/sso_user_info.jsp?returl="+returl;
    var logout_url = "https://membership.chosun.com/login/logout.jsp?returl="+returl;
    var regist_url = "https://membership.chosun.com/join/registUser.jsp?site=chosun";
    var join_url = "https://membership.chosun.com/join/registUser.jsp?act=myindex&site=chosun";
    var idpw_url = "https://membership.chosun.com/join/registUser.jsp?act=idpw&site=chosun";
    var logStr;

    var logLink = document.getElementById("logLink");
    var memberLink = document.getElementById("memberLink");

    //로그인여부 - 쿠키값 확인
    if (GetAuthCookie('SMSESSION')=="" || GetAuthCookie('SMSESSION') == "LOGGEDOFF" || GetAuthCookie('SM_USER') =="") {
        logLink.href = login_url;
        logLink.innerHTML = "로그인";
        memberLink.href = regist_url;
        memberLink.innerHTML = "회원가입";
    }
    else if (GetAuthCookie('dz_nm')=="" || GetAuthCookie('dz_info')=="") {
    var relogin_url = "https://membership.chosun.com/login/protect_sso/sso_user_info.jsp?returl="+returl;
        parent.location.href = relogin_url;
    } else {
        logLink.href = logout_url;
        logLink.innerHTML = "로그아웃";
        memberLink.href = join_url;
        memberLink.innerHTML = "정보수정";
    }
    return logStr;
}
loginFrame();
</script>

      <script>
        function edito_roll() {
          var now = new Date();
          var hour = now.getHours();
          if (hour.toString().length == 1) {
            var hour = '0' + hour;
          }
          var edito = document.querySelectorAll('#opi_01_id .news_item');
          var edito_count = edito.length;
          if (edito_count == 3) {
            //console.log('3개네요!');
            if (hour % 3 == 0) {
              edito[0].style.display = "table-cell";
              edito[1].style.display = "none";
              edito[2].style.display = "none";
            } else if (hour % 3 == 1) {
              edito[0].style.display = "none";
              edito[1].style.display = "table-cell";
              edito[2].style.display = "none";
            } else if (hour % 3 == 2) {
              edito[0].style.display = "none";
              edito[1].style.display = "none";
              edito[2].style.display = "table-cell";
            } else {
              return false;
            }
          } else if (edito_count == 2) {
            //console.log('2개네요!');
            if (hour % 2 == 0) {
              edito[0].style.display = "table-cell";
              edito[1].style.display = "none";
            } else if (hour % 2 == 1) {
              edito[0].style.display = "none";
              edito[1].style.display = "table-cell";
            } else {
              return false;
            }
          } else if (edito_count == 1) {
            //console.log('1개네요!');
            edito[0].style.display = "table-cell";
          } else if (edito_count >= 4) {
            //console.log('4개가 넘네요!');
            for (var i = 0, length = edito_count; i < length; i++) {
              edito[i].style.display = "none";
              edito[0].style.display = "table-cell";
            }
          } else {
            return false;
          }
        }

        function edito_roll2() {
          var now = new Date();
          var hour = now.getSeconds();
          if (hour.toString().length == 1) {
            var hour = '0' + hour;
          }
          var edito = document.querySelectorAll('#opi_02_id .news_item');
          var edito_count = edito.length;
          if (edito_count == 3) {
            //console.log('3개네요!');
            if (hour % 3 == 0) {
              edito[0].style.display = "none";
              edito[1].style.display = "table-cell";
              edito[2].style.display = "none";
            } else if (hour % 3 == 1) {
              edito[0].style.display = "none";
              edito[1].style.display = "none";
              edito[2].style.display = "table-cell";
            } else if (hour % 3 == 2) {
              edito[0].style.display = "table-cell";
              edito[1].style.display = "none";
              edito[2].style.display = "none";
            } else {
              return false;
            }
          } else if (edito_count == 2) {
            //console.log('2개네요!');
            if (hour % 2 == 0) {
              edito[0].style.display = "none";
              edito[1].style.display = "table-cell";
            } else if (hour % 2 == 1) {
              edito[0].style.display = "table-cell";
              edito[1].style.display = "none";
            } else {
              return false;
            }
          } else if (edito_count == 1) {
            //console.log('1개네요!');
            edito[0].style.display = "table-cell";
          } else if (edito_count >= 4) {
            //console.log('4개가 넘네요!');
            for (var i = 0, length = edito_count; i < length; i++) {
              edito[i].style.display = "none";
              edito[1].style.display = "table-cell";
            }
          } else {
            return false;
          }
        }

        //edito_roll()
        edito_roll2()
      </script>

$(document).ready(function () {

    if ( cookiedata.indexOf("search_tip_cook=on") > -1 ) {
    //console.log('쿠키에서 닫기로 설정!');
    return;
    };
    // var searchTip = $('#csh_search_tip_id');

    searchTipto.after('<div class="csh_search_tip vis" id="csh_search_tip_id"> <img src="https://image.chosun.com/main/banner/cs_top_search_tip.png" alt=""> <button class="csh_search_tip_close" id="csh_search_tip_close_id">닫기</button> </div>');

    $('#csh_search_id, #csh_search_tip_close_id').on('click', function () {
      var searchTip = $('#csh_search_tip_id'),
          btnID = $(this).attr('id');
        if ( btnID == 'csh_search_tip_close_id' ) {
            setCookie( "search_tip_cook", "on" , 24 );
            searchTip.removeClass('vis');
        } else {
            searchTip.removeClass('vis');
        }  
    });   

  });
</script>

<script>
//common function
function setCookie( name, value, expirehours ) {
    var todayDate = new Date(); 
    todayDate.setHours( todayDate.getHours() + expirehours ); 
    document.cookie = name + "=" + escape( value ) + "; path=/; expires=" + todayDate.toGMTString() + ";" 
};
cookiedata = document.cookie; 

$(document).ready(function () {
if ( cookiedata.indexOf("cs_fact_cook=on") > -1 ) {
  //console.log('쿠키에서 닫기로 설정!');
  return;
};
    $('#cen_close_txt_id, #cen_close_btn_id').on('click', function (e) {
        e.preventDefault();
        $('#cen_pop_id').removeClass('vis');
    });
    $('#cen_close_check_id').on('click', function (e) {
      e.preventDefault();
      $('#cen_pop_id').removeClass('vis');
      setCookie( "cs_fact_cook", "on" , 120 );
    });

    //cen pop run
    //console.log( new Date() );
    
    if ( new Date() >= new Date('10/10/2019 03:00:00') && new Date() < new Date('10/10/2019 23:59:00')) {
        $('#cen_pop_id').addClass('vis');
        //console.log('목표 시간 내!');
    } else {
        //console.log('목표 시간 외입니다!');
    }  
});
</script>

        var sendPageLoadEvent = function () {

                if (!!hepsiBus && timing) {
